ESFM v0.5 NUM

Note: This is still a very early look into the unfinished text of the Open English Translation of the Bible. Please double-check the text before using in public. Some things (like capitalisation of “him” referring to Jesus or “father” referring to God) in the RV haven’t been decided yet so we’re still testing both ways.

Note: The Readers’ Version on the left is a translation into contemporary English aimed at the person on the street who hasn’t necessarily been brought up with exposure to Biblical jargon and/or King James English. It’s designed to be used alongside the Literal Version on the right which gives the English reader a window into what’s actually written in the original languages. (See the introduction for more details—we recommend that you read the introduction first if you’re wanting to fully understand the Literal Version.) By comparing the left and right columns, you should be able to easily get the message of the text, while at the same time keeping an eye on what it was actually translated from.

Numbers

It is our prayer that the Open English Translation of the Bible will give you clear understanding of the messages written by the inspired Biblical writers.

Introduction

The baseen te Numiru migpangguhud concerning the descendants of Israel seled te hep‑at pulu (40) leg‑un puun te peg-awe dan te Bubungan Sinay, taman te migginguma sikandan diye te igsile te tane insaad te God igbehey kandan. The ngaran te seini baseen, due kalabetan te amana impurtanti baad te seini pangguhuren iyan ka pegpanlista of Muwisis te descendants of Israel diye te Bubungan Sinay te ware pad sikandan mig-awe diye. Peglihad te hep‑at pulu (40) leg‑un, inggimu e man‑e ka pegpanlista diye te Muwab, dapit te igsile te Weyig Hurdan. Te elat-elat te seini se kararuwa pegpanlista te keet-etawan, miggendiye ka descendants of Israel te Kadis-Barniya te igkakawanan balabahan eletanan te Kanaan. Piru puun te Kadis-Barniya, ware sikandan nakaseled te tane insaad te God igbehey kandan. Peglihad te masulug me leg‑un te peg-ugpe dan te seeye inged, miggendiye sikandan te tane dapit te igsile te Weyig Hurdan. The sabeka punduk te keet-etawan mig-ugpe diye, and ka duma miglapas te Weyig Hurdan peendiye te Kanaan.

The baseen te Numiru migpangguhud man‑e concerning the keet-etawan layun naawei te kabagget, nenaaldek taliware te kalised, and migsukul te God and ki Muwisis in-alam te God eyew iyan egpangulu kandan. Migpangguhud man‑e seini concerning the pegkamatinumanen te God and te pegsagman din te keet-etawan din ware egtamanan minsan pad nenaawaan sikandan te kabagget, and migmasinupaken. Migpangguhud man‑e seini concerning the kene egkataman pegpamakey of Muwisis te God and te keet-etawan din minsan pad te due me timpu naaminan sikandin te pegpariralem.

Main components of this “book”

The pegpangandam te descendants of Israel te pegligkat te Sinay 1:1-9:23

a. The hun‑a pegpanlista of Muwisis te descendants of Israel 1:1-4:49

b. The nalein-lein me balaud and me tulumanen 5:1-8:26

c. The igkarangeb Sahakeen te Peglihad te Panalihan 9:1-23

Puun te Bubungan Sinay peendiye te Muwab 10:1-21:35

The neneyitabu diye te Muwab 22:1-32:42

The me inged nabayaan te descendants of Israel 33:1-49

Me paney-paney te ware pad miglapas te Hurdan 33:50-36:13

See also the FAQs and the Glossary.
